# 商机(deal) :id=deal
## 创建商机

<el-row>
<div style="width: 80px">
<el-alert center title="POST" style="background-color: rgba(52, 143, 228, 0.1);color: #348fe4;" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
<div style="margin-left:5px;width: calc(100% - 85px)">
<el-alert title="/deals" type="info" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
</el-row>
权限标识：`CREATE`



##### 请求参数 {docsify-ignore}

|<el-row justify="space-between"><el-col :span="20">executors</el-col><el-col :span="4" style="text-align:right"><el-text size="small" type="success">可选</el-text></el-col> </el-row>|Object|执行人|

## 获取商机

<el-row>
<div style="width: 80px">
<el-alert center title="GET" type="success" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
<div style="margin-left:5px;width: calc(100% - 85px)">
<el-alert title="/deals/{key}" type="info" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
</el-row>
权限标识：`READ`

##### 路径参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
|key|String|标识|




##### 响应示例： {docsify-ignore}
```json

{
  "account_name" : null,
  "executors" : null,
  "validity" : null,
  "business_line" : null,
  "last_assess_time" : null,
  "stage_probability" : null,
  "account_id" : null,
  "amount" : null,
  "attachments" : null,
  "change_log_time_s" : null,
  "closing_date" : null,
  "contact_id" : null,
  "contact_name" : null,
  "create_man" : null,
  "create_time" : null,
  "deal_name" : null,
  "description" : null,
  "expected_revenue" : null,
  "id" : null,
  "last_activity_time" : null,
  "lead_conversion_time" : null,
  "lead_source" : null,
  "locked_s" : null,
  "name" : null,
  "next_step" : null,
  "overall_sales_duration" : null,
  "owner" : null,
  "probability" : null,
  "reason_for_loss_s" : null,
  "sales_cycle_duration" : null,
  "stage" : null,
  "tag" : null,
  "type" : null,
  "update_man" : null,

}
```

## 添加商机

<el-row>
<div style="width: 80px">
<el-alert center title="POST" style="background-color: rgba(52, 143, 228, 0.1);color: #348fe4;" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
<div style="margin-left:5px;width: calc(100% - 85px)">
<el-alert title="/deals/add_deal" type="info" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
</el-row>
权限标识：`NONE`



##### 请求参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|

## 根据客户下载导入模板

</div>
<div style="margin-left:5px;width: calc(100% - 85px)">
<el-alert title="/accounts/{pkey}/deals/importtemplate" type="info" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
</el-row>


##### 路径参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
|pkey|String|标识|

##### 查询参数 {docsify-ignore}

|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
| srfimporttag | String | 导入标识 |



## 根据客户数据导出

<el-row>
<div style="width: 80px">
<el-alert center title="POST" style="background-color: rgba(52, 143, 228, 0.1);color: #348fe4;" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
<div style="margin-left:5px;width: calc(100% - 85px)">
<el-alert title="/accounts/{pkey}/deals/exportdata/{param},/accounts/{pkey}/deals/exportdata/{param}/{key}" type="info" :closable="false" ></el-alert>
</div>
</el-row>

##### 路径参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
|pkey|String|标识|
|param|String|导出集合方法名称|
|key|String|数据主键|

##### 查询参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
|key|String|标识|
|srfexporttag|String|导出模板标识|

##### 请求参数 {docsify-ignore}
|字段col300|类型col150|备注col400|
|---|---|----|
|page|Integer|page|
|size|Integer|分页大小|
|n_xxx_eq|String|过滤参数|
